1b2(tog gzungs): ya da su twa/ bad skad do// 'phags pa 'dus pa da pe che tig gi
1b3(tog gzungs): da daM/ 'phags pa 'dus pa re pa
1b4(tog gzungs): gzung si zhes bya ba theg pa ched po'i mdo// de bzhi gshegs pa 'odagan
2a1(tog gzungs): spos sdang dpal la phyag 'tshal lo// tshangs pa rte dpe dbang
2a2(tog gzungs): na la bag 'tshal lo// de dag la phyag 'tshal te/ bdad kyi 'khor gyi sa mi chags
2a3(tog gzungs): pa zhes bya ba'i kadang pa 'di skor ba rab gyis// bdag gi rigs sngags 'di sdus pa na
2b1(tog gzungs): cig/ 'di lta ste/ ang na me/ ang na me/ sa pa ri pa ri ke/ tsa ni ta ba ska ma hA dza/ kha ma kha ya/ i li mi li/ gi li mi li

2b3(tog gzungs): ma'i tshal/ byA ka lan ta ka na gnas pa la dge slong stong du tshang ba'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang / dgra bcom
2b4(tog gzungs): bzag pazad pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa/ dbang du gyur pa/ sems shin du rnam par grol ba/ shes rab shin du rnam
3a1(tog gzungs): par grol ba/ cang shes pa/ glang po chen po bya ba byas pa/ byed pa byas pa/ khur bor ba/ bdag gi don rjes su thob
3a2(tog gzungs): pa/ srad pa kun du sbyor ba yongs su zad pa/ yang dag pa'i sems shin du rnam par grol ba/ sems can gyi dbang thams cad
3a3(tog gzungs): kyi dam pa'i pha rol du son pa dang / sha stag dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' khri'i byang chub sems dpa
3a4(tog gzungs): dge 'dun chen po 'di lta ste/ lhun po rtse 'dzin gzhon nur gyur pa dang / chu lha'i blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa dang / bzang skyong ni
3b1(tog gzungs): blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo// rgyal po'i blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa dang // 'od kyi blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa dang
3b2(tog gzungs): nam mkha'i blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa dang / nam mkha'i blo gros gzhon nur gyur pa do/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang
3b3(tog gzungs): thub dka' gzhon nur pa dang / chu lha gzhon nur gyur pa dang / dri ma med pa gzhon nur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems
3b4(tog gzungs): dpa' chen po byams pa dang / de dag la sogs pa khri thams cad dang / gzungs dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / thob pa chos thams
3b5(tog gzungs): cad la sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes can// sems can thams cad la sems mnyam pa/ bdud kyi yul thams cad las yang
5a1(tog gzungs): dag par 'das pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la 'jug pa/ shes pa la mkhas pa byams pa chen po dang / 
5a2(tog gzungs): rje chen po dang ldan pa/ thabs shes pa la mkhas pa/ sha stag dag dang / yang thabs gcig go// de'i tshe rgyal po'i khab kyi gong khyer chen pos/ 
5a3(tog gzungs): kun du rgyu mkhas pa gsal ba yid gzhungs pa/ rig pa'i gnas bco brgyad kyi pha rol du son pa/ g.yog lnga brgya pa/ gcig gi ming ni nye rgyal/ 
5a4(tog gzungs): gcig ni ming ni pang nas skye zhes bya ba gnyis zhig 'khod de/ tshogs kyi gtso bo g.yog gi tshogs can de gnyis phan tshun 'di ltar bdag cag las
5a5(tog gzungs): gang gis thog mar bdud rtsi thob pa des/ gcig la gcig sbran/ zhes dam tshig byas so// de nas tshe dang ldan pa rta thul snga gro'i dus kyi tshe/ sham thabs
5b1(tog gzungs): chos pos bgos/ lhung zed thogs nas/ rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por bsod snyoms kyi phyir bzhugs pa dang / kun du rgya nye rgyal gyis tshe dang ldan pa
5b2(tog gzungs): thal de lta bur spyod yul du zhugs nas rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por bsod snyoms kyi phyir song ba mthong ngo // mthong nas de 'di snyam du sems te/ ji lnga
5b3(tog gzungs): dge slong 'dri'i spyod la mi mdzes pa/ 'di lta bu ni bdag gis sngon chad dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze 'am/ mir gyur pa su la yang gang yang sngon ma mthong na/ bdag de'i
5b4(tog gzungs): gan du song ste/ tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyi ston pa gang yin/ gang las rab tu byung / gang gis chos la dga' zhes 'dri'o snyom mo// de nas kun du rgya nya rgyal tshe dang ldan pa tsa
5b5(tog gzungs): dal gi la der dong sde tshe dang ldan pa rta thul dang lhan cig tu mngon du yang dag par dga' bar bya ba dang / yang dag par mgu bar bya ba'i phyir// gtam sna tshogs byas
5b6(tog gzungs): gas gcig tu 'dug go// phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas kyang kun du rgya nye rgyal gyis/ tshe dang ldan pa rta thul la 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyi ston pa
6a1(tog gzungs): 'di ma na gang las rab tu byung / glang gi chos la drug rtsod pa / sprul gyis/ kun gyigyi rgyal ma 'di skad ces smras/ kya'i sras rlo su la shugs dka
6a2(tog gzungs): na po kun gyi dbang ldan pa// 'khor po'i rgya mtsho pha rol byin cing grol la de bzhin 'gro ba skyo lho mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas shes bya sod mdzod mi mnyam sreg pa
6a3(tog gzungs): daltar 'odi ni yod// dri ma med pa de'i skyabs su song ste nga ni de'i chos la dga'// nye rgyal gyis smras pa/ khyod kyi ston pa ci ska da sgra ci ska ston// tshe 'i/ 
6a4(tog gzungs): smras pa/ de'i phyir tshe dang ldan pa legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang ngas bshad do// ji ltar 'jig rten las dang nyon mongs rgyur bces byed rgyu che ma
6a5(tog gzungs): las dang nyon mongs pa dag ldog rgyu de yang 'dren pas rab tu gsungs// gang na skyo dang dga' dang rgad pa'i sdug bsngal ngos phyir mi gnas pa na/ thur pa'i/ 
6a6(tog gzungs): de yis rung gis gsungs// de nas kun de rgyu nye rgyal gyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di thos nas/ chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdug med cing dri ma dang bral la nyon mo
6a7(tog gzungs): skyes te/ des rgyun dri zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob nas/ de'i tshe tshogs su bcad pa 'di skad ces smraso// sangs rgyas kyis ni shin du rnyede dka' bris gter bdud rtsi'i chos
6b1(tog gzungs): 'di ni rtagra tu skye ba'i 'brang chu skyems par bden par khong du chud/ de ni 'gro ba rnams kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar 'gyur te/ lam 'di dam phra shes rab chos rnams bsgom pa
6b2(tog gzungs): mnyam byed pa yin// de nas kun du rgyu nye rgyal gyis tshe dang ldan pa tu thul la 'di skad ces smras// tshe dang ldan pa de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs bya
6b3(tog gzungs): sangs rgyas de dag lta ga la bzhugs// tshe dang ldan pa rta thul gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ni rgyal po'i khab 'od mi'i tshu la bya ka lan ta ka gnas pa ni/ 'di
6b4(tog gzungs): lnga ste ral pa can stong rab tu byung ba'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang thabs gcig tu zhugs// rgyal gyis smras pa/ bdag gis glo gos po'i mchog dang slob ma'i
6b5(tog gzungs): 'khor la braltas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thad du rab tu byung ngo // de nas kun du rgyu nye rgyal che dang ldan pa rta thul gyi rkang pa la mgo bos phyag 'tsha
6b6(tog gzungs): skor ba byas te slar song nas/ kun du rgyu pang nas skyes gal ba der song ba mthong nas/ kun du rgyu pang nas rmi skyes kyis kun du rgyu nye rgyal rgyang ring po nas 'ong bu mthu
6b7(tog gzungs): na du rgyu nye rgyal la 'di skad ces smos so// tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyi dbang po rnams ni dngasau/ bzhin gyi mdangos ni yongs su dag/ 
7a1(tog gzungs): bye las blta sa na/ tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyis bdud rtsi rnyed do/ nye rgyal gyis smras pa tshe dang ldan pa de de bzhin te/ kho bos bdud rtsi rnyed kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa
7a2(tog gzungs): su par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shog dang / kho bos ji snyed pa khyod la bshad do// de nas kun du rgyu bong nas skyes stan lnga sa langs nas/ bla gos breg pa
7a3(tog gzungs): zur te/ pu snga mo g.yas pa'i lha ngas la btsugs nas/ kun du rgyu nye rgyal ga la ba de log suM thal mo sbyar ba btud nas 'di skad ces smra so// gang gis sri
7a4(tog gzungs): gsum rgya mtsho myur rga la rdzing // phung po dgra chen rnam par ba shig bya ba// mya dran med ni lam de shod cig dang // yang 'byung med pa'i lam du 'jug par bya// de nas
7a5(tog gzungs): kun du rgyu nye rgyal gyis 'di skad ces smras so// ji ltar 'jig rten las dang nyon mongs rgyur bcas ber rgyu ldan 'byung dang // lus dang nyon mongs pa dag ldog rgyu de yang
7a6(tog gzungs): 'dren pas rab tu gsungs// gang ni skye dang rga dang rgud pa'i sdug bsngal nges par mi gnas pa// thor bu'i mchog dri skye bri'i khyi mchog dri yis rang gis mkhyen to gsungs
7a7(tog gzungs): pa de nas skyes kyis smras pa/ sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar bya tI phyir dri me med pa zhi ba'i chos// nyon mongs ltas ngani nyeso ba thams cad zhi byed mi shes gcod pa dang / 'di na
7b1(tog gzungs): 'dus pas gseg gsob de phyir stong pa smra bar thub pas gsungs// de bas zhi bar de 'gyur dri ma med pa'i tshig de zlos te gsungs/ nye rgyal gyis smras pa/ ji ltar
7b2(tog gzungs): 'jig rten las dang nyon mongs pargyur bces byed rgyur ldan 'byung dang // las dang nyon mongs pa drag ldog rgyu de yang 'dren pa skye rab tu gsungs/ gdun skye dang rga dang
7b3(tog gzungs): rgud pa'i sdug bsngal nyes par mi gnas pa// thar pa'i mchog de smra ba'i khyu mchog de yis rang gis mi khyen te gsung so// do nas kun du rgyu ba nas skyes kyi/ de nyid
7b4(tog gzungs): chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdul med cing dri ma dang bral la// nyon mongs pa med pa rnam par sbyangs te// de rgyun du zhigs pa'i 'bras bu thib nasa'adi skad ces
7b5(tog gzungs): smra so/ yang dag spyod pa 'di ni chu bo sgrol ba bzhi pa mgyogs pa'i gzings// ye shes mchog 'dri sdug bsngal gsum po zhi byed 'khor bI'i pha rol 'gro/ 'di ni yang
7b6(tog gzungs): shes na nyon mongs bang po 'jom zhing btud 'dul 'gyur// thar pa 'di ni dgra dang 'thab mo bskul cing sdug bsngal rgya mtsho snyoms// phyung nas skyes kyis smras pad+ma bcom
7b7(tog gzungs): ldan 'das de bzhin gshogs pa dge bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de de ltar gal bzhugs/ nye rgyal gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa bdag gis bcom
7'a1(tog gzungs): ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen po'i 'od ma'i tshal bya ka lan ta ka gnas pa na/ dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge
7'a2(tog gzungs): bye dang / ba sa gcig tu zhugs shes thos nas// bdag cag gnyis bcom ldan 'das de'i thad du rab tu byung ngam/ byeng nas skyes kyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan
7'a3(tog gzungs): bzhin te/ bdag cig gi 'khor la bltas la rab tu 'byung ngo // de nas kun du rgyu nye rgya la dang bang nas skyes ring go'i khor ga le ba der dadzo / de nas skad cig
7'a4(tog gzungs): yud tsamadol// bdud sdig can gyis yul ang ga ming gi d+ha na/ mkhas shing sbyin pa dang / brjod pa dang grags bai ri ldan pa/ skyes bu dam pa nye rgyal dang bra
7'a5(tog gzungs): ge yog dang btsos te/ dge slong ke'u te ma'i snyan pa la rab tu 'byung bar 'dod do/ zhes thos nas de 'di snyam du sems so// kyi rgyud de gnyis gal te/ dges
7'a6(tog gzungs): ma slob mar gyur na/ bdag gi bdud kyi yul stongs par byed kyis bdag der song ste/ skyes bu dam pa de gnyis rab tu 'byung ba las bzlog la sdig can gyi lta ba la
7'a7(tog gzungs): gago snyam ste/ de nas skad cig thang cig yud tsamo dal/ bdud sdig can myur du bdog gi khang pa nas mi snang bar byas te/ tshe dang ldan pa rta thul gyi cha byed dang
7'b1(tog gzungs): drang sprod lam du bsgyur nas/ skyes bu dam pa de gnyis kyi mdun na la ma gar 'dug ste/ kho bos sngar smras rgyu dang byed rgyu lta bu de ni log pa ste/ khyed gnyis yid kyi spyod pa
7'b2(tog gzungs): ci la nges par bags par bya ba'i phyir// smras pa de dag thams cad don yod ma yin 'di la rgyu yang med/ dge dang mo dge'i las de'i 'bras bu thob pa 'di na ga la yod/ myur
7'b3(tog gzungs): du khyed gnyis 'dod pa'i yon tan rnams la rab skyed rtsed mo byed/ spyi dga' na mchi med cing sdug bsngal med cing 'jig rten pa rol med/ bsod nams bsod nams
7'b4(tog gzungs): man las bskyed 'bras med rgyu dang byed pa med/ rnyed phyir 'di ni shAkya'i bu yis smras kyis dad pa sem 'gro shig/ de nas te tshul dang bang nas skyes 'di snyam du sems
7'b5(tog gzungs): kyem bdud sdig ca na badrug tsug rab tu 'byung ba lus zlog pa'i phyir 'angs sa snyam nas/ de nas nye rgyal chub kyis phyogs te/ 'dug nas rang gi 'khor la bros te'ang
7'b6(tog gzungs): skad ces smras/ bram ze'i khe'u nyon cig 'khor ba'i skyo ni// dran por gyis la 'jig rten dga' gzir cing 'chi bdag gis ni rab bskor ba/ de gnyis spang phyir rab byung theg
7'b7(tog gzungs): par bzu // de na se byung na so skyes kyis bdad la slar smras pa// mkhas pa blo 'chang sdug bsngal gsum mthar 'byin mchog chos rnams kun shes kyiso// rnam pa kan du
10a1(tog gzungs): bdag kyang cang mi zer bar 'khod do// yang glu rab tu blangs shing sil snyan byas pa dang / bdud sdig can gyis lag pa gnyis g.yabs ste bos so// lha'i bu mo de
10a2(tog gzungs): dag gis dga' ba dang ldan pa'i glu dang / gar dang sil snyan lan bdun gyi bar du byas pa dang / yang de bzhin du bdud sdig can de/ lag pa gnyis bsgreng nas 'bad cing / sgra ma
10a3(tog gzungs): byed ma byed ces zer ro// de skad ces smras pa dang / lha'i bu mo de dag cang mi zer bar 'khod de// de nas lha'i bu mi dbyings snyan klog ces bya bas// bdud sdig can ka lwa ba de legs
10a4(tog gzungs): thal mo sbyar ba btud nas 'di skad ces smras so// gtso bo khyod kyis deng 'dir 'chi 'pho ltas shig gzigs sam ci// 'on kyang ci zhig de ring 'gro ba zhugs kyis 'khrugs gyur
10a5(tog gzungs): tam/ 'on te 'di na khyod dag stobs chen 'ga' zhig mchis lags sam/ ci'i slad du khyod ni dges par mi zhugs thugs ngan mdzad/ bdud kyis smras pa// nga la dag yod pa ni
10a6(tog gzungs): stobs ldan sems thul ba/ sa stengs shAkya'i bu po sgyum bslabs pa'i blo// de ni ci nas gal te brlag par ma gyur na/ de yis nga yi 'dod khams 'di ni stongs par byed// lha'i
10a7(tog gzungs): bu des smras pa/ gtso bo srid gsum bcings srid rgya mtsho'i mtha' rings la// zad babyed nus pa'i stobs dang ldan pa su zhig mchis/ bdag po thabs stobs brtson 'grus
10b1(tog gzungs): rtsal rnams gang gis kyang // de la de ring ma lus bgyis par nus ma mchis/ bdud kyis smras pa/ sbyin dang brtul zhugs bsam pa smon lam snying rje'i zhabs pa can/ sdong ba mtshan
10b2(tog gzungs): ma med pa'i mtshon cha mchog dang gzhu thogs te/ 'khor ba las byung rab tu zhi ba'i lam dang 'thun gyur nas// srid pa ma lus bzlog pa nye bar bstan par byed pa po/ de'i slob
10b3(tog gzungs): ma bsam gtan la ni mngon par brtson yid kyis// dben par rgyu zhing nyes pa zad par bya phyir khor yug tu/ cho ga bzhin du zhugs nas grong dang grong khyer stong pa dang // nags kyi/ 
10b4(tog gzungs): nang dag dang ni ri'i sman ljongs rnams na gnas// rdzu 'phrul dang ni stobs dang snying rje'i grogs dang ldan pa yi// dam pa nye rgyal pang nas skyes gnyis thub pas pa tAl bar 'gyur/ 
10b5(tog gzungs): rab btul chos can 'jig rten gsum kun cho ga bzhin du btul/ des ni nga'i 'dod khams 'di dag stongs par byed par 'gyur/ de nas bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya po de dag gis
10b6(tog gzungs): bdud sdig can las bcom ldan 'das kyi yon tan gyi sngags pa thos nas/ thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin rnam pa dang bral ba'i klog ces bya ba thob bo// 
10b7(tog gzungs): de nas bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya po de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir lha'i sil snyan dang / me tog dang / gdugs dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / lha/ 
11a1(tog gzungs): rtsub dang / skud pa dang / rgyun de dag bcom ldan 'das gal ba de log su gtor ba dang / lha'i me tog dang sim snyan nas brgyan gyi bar du/ de dag bcom ldan
11a2(tog gzungs): 'das kyis rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang mthus 'od ma 'a tshal du bab par gyur to// bdud kyi bu mo de dag kyang g.yog dang bas so so nas bcom ldan 'das mthong ngo // de dag gis mthong nas
11a3(tog gzungs): kyang rab tu dga' ba dang / rangs pa skyes par gyur to// gang gi phyir 'od ma'i tshil du 'di lta bu me tog gi char rab tu bab ces/ dge slong de dag the tsom skyes nas/ bcom ldan 'das
11a4(tog gzungs): kyis shA ro'i bu dang me'u 'gal gyi bu g.yog dang bcas pa 'di gnyis la ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba/ sngon mthong ma thos pa'i me tog gi char rab tu bab pa lags/ bcom ldan
11a5(tog gzungs): 'das 'di'i rgyu ci lags rkyen gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ rigs kyi bu 'di gnyis kyi mthu ma yin te/ bdud sdig can gyi g.yog mo lnga brgya
11a6(tog gzungs): tsam gyis/ bdud kyi khang pa de nas nga la mchod pa'i bye ba'i phyir/ 'di lta ba'i me tog gi char chen po nas rgyan gyi bar gyi char phab po// de dag ring po mi thogs par 'dir
11a7(tog gzungs): 'ongs te/ nga las bla na med pa yang dag par lakhang bsen pa thob po// de nas bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya blo de dag so so nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung
11b1(tog gzungs): dang brjod pa'i dbyangs thos nas/ bcom ldan 'das la de bas kyang rab tu dga' ba skyes nas de dag dga' ba dang bde ba dang rangs pa des/ byang chub kyi sems mi brjed pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin
11b2(tog gzungs): thob bo// de nas yang bdud kyi bu mo de dag bdud kyi khang pa der gos phrag pa gcig tu dgos te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das phyogs
11b3(tog gzungs): gang na bzhugs pa'i phyogs der bltas nas/ 'di skad ces gsol to// sred cha me lus skyems pa 'gro ba'i mig cig pa/ mig ma mchis pa'i 'jig rten kun la gzigs nas ni// khyod
11b4(tog gzungs): der lha dang mir bcas pa yi 'gro ba sgrol// thub pa bdag cag ji ltar myur du sa nges rgyas gyur/ lha dang mis mchod don dam gsung ba bcom ldan 'das/ bdag cag 'thun par bud med slad
11b5(tog gzungs): pa nyid spangs nas/ blo mchog khyed kyi 'phrul gyis drung du myur bar ni// mchis nas ni bzhin thub pa'i dbang po'i gsung nyan to// bdag med gsung ba don dam gzigs pa bcom ldan
11b6(tog gzungs): 'das/ byang chub yan lag rin chen dri med nor gsung sgron/ mtshungs med bdud kyi stobs btul khyod kyis bdag cag la// da ltar myur du lhan cig byang chub lung bstan
11b7(tog gzungs): gsol/ de nas bdud kyi bu mo de dag stan langs te mgrin cig tu/ bdud sdig can la 'di skad ces smras so// nyes byas blo gros can khyod snying po mi g.yo ba'o// dpal rnyed ji phyir/ 
12a1(tog gzungs): bcom ldan 'das la sdang bar sems// dregs pas gos nas skye ba la sogs sdug bsngal gyis// lus kun gtses te mi zad gan su nye bar song / 
12a2(tog gzungs): de ltar khro ba spangs te rgyal ba dad par gyis// 'khor ba'i nges par dregs pa'i 'dam las thar de'i bdag/ 'di ni nyid kyis 'gro ba kun gyi ngo bo nyid/ thugs rje can
12a3(tog gzungs): gyi skyabasu 'dong gis myur du bzhud// de nas bdud sdig can shin du gdag pa'i yid dang ldan pa 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis 'di 'dra bdud kyi stobs kyi yul drag
12a4(tog gzungs): po dran par byas la/ gang gi yog lnga brgya tsam po de dge bdag nyid bo cing baM lngas bcings par mthong bar byas te/ 'di nas bzlog la 'gro mi nus par bya'o snyam pa dang / 
12a5(tog gzungs): bdud des de dag bcing ma nus so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar g.yog mo lnga brgya tsam po de dag de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs po'i phyir ro// de nas g.yog
12a6(tog gzungs): mo lnga brgya tsam po de dag phyi bdud sdig can gyi drung nas dong ba dang / de nas bdud sdig can rab tu 'khros te/ de 'di snyam du sems bdag gis yang 'di 'dra ba'i bdud kyi stongs
12a7(tog gzungs): kyi yul drag po dran par byas te ci nas bdag gi g.yog mo de dang phyogs dang phyogs 'tshams thams cad 'khrul nas dge slong go'u ta ma mi mthong zhing slar yang bdag gi
12b1(tog gzungs): gan su 'ong bar na mkha' 'di dag thams cad du/ rnam par mthor rlung dang / rlung nag po chen pos kun khyab par bya'o snyam na yang mang rgyas kyi byin gyi brlangs kyi mthu stobs
12b2(tog gzungs): kyis rlung zad kyang langs par byed ma nus so// the ne skra'i rtse mo gcig tsam yang skyong ma nus na mang de lta ci smos// de nas yang bdud sdig can rab tu 'khros shing / stu gri sngal
12b3(tog gzungs): de yid mi bde zhing yid la bcags nas ngu zhing skad chen pos rang gi bu dang tshogs kyi 'khor la bos te/ bdud kyi gnas thams cang sgras gang bar bya so// sdug pa'i bu
12b4(tog gzungs): dang tshogs kyi 'khor rnams tshur shog cig/ nga ni bdag yul rang gi rdzu 'phrul stobs las nyams// shAkya'i ba 'di rgya ldan g.yon can dag 'jam lo// khong nas rang bzhin
12b5(tog gzungs): dug sdong 'dra ba 'dir skyes te/ de nas sgra des bdud kyi g.yo ga mo dang / bdud kyi bu mo de dag thams cad dang / bdud kyi ni tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa thams cad rings
12b6(tog gzungs): pa'i gzugs kyis myur du lhags nas/ bdud sdig can gyi mdun du 'khod pa dang / 'khor de'i nang du bdud kyi bu rgyal ba'i blo gros zhes bya ba des thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces
12b7(tog gzungs): smra so// ci'i slad du thugs 'khros rab tu 'khrugs shing thugs mi dges// sreg bskal deng 'dir mi byung 'di nas khyod ma 'phos// 'di ni khyod lhag sgra ni su yang ma mchis
13a1(tog gzungs): na/ khyad rmongs par gyur tam ci smad gzhan du dgongs// bdud kyis smras pa/ shAkya'i bu po dmangs pal shing gi grib ma 'dug pa ma mthong ngam/ ci phyir khyod na
13a2(tog gzungs): mdun du stabs dang ldan pa'i sgra med smras// stobs cig ldan pa g.yon can de yis thams cad rnam pa du mar smras/ bdag cag pu dang sder me lce 'bar dang bcas pas mes yis
13a3(tog gzungs): bsregs/ 'jig rten 'di na skyes bu gtso ba dpal dang brjod pa rnam grags pa/ mkhas pastan bcos snyan dang gis mang po byed brtson 'thun pa myur bar yang // chos kyi skyo ba tang gi
13a4(tog gzungs): btang gis drangs te shAkya'i bu 'di'i skyabs der song // lus mdzes g.yon can blo gros ldan 'di'i nga'i dgrar ni rab tu gnan// rab tu sdug pa'i g.yog mo de dge snying rje med par dra
13a5(tog gzungs): bor te// nga la dbang gtsugs nas ni de ring dge sbyong de'i skyab su song // gal te bdag cag myur bsgri bas stobs chen 'di dang thal bar ma byas ni// g.yo dang rgyu yis srid pa gsum po
13a6(tog gzungs): de dag ma lus stongs par byed// de nas bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag thams cad kyis thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so// de ltar bgyi'o bdag cag gi rdzu 'phrul
13a7(tog gzungs): dang / stobs kyi yul ni mthu dang rnam par sprul pa de dag thams cad stan de/ shAkya'i bu 'di dag gal te thal bar bgyi nus pa lhan ni legs// de ltar ma nus na ni de'i skyab su mchis
13b1(tog gzungs): yab nyid kyis mngon sum du gyur pa lags te/ gang bdag cag sde chen pos yongasu bskor ba/ sngar shAkya'i bu gcig pu gnyi su med pa 'dis// rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs kyis rab tu 'pham par bgyis
13b2(tog gzungs): na/ ngagayog mang bar gyur pa lta ci smos// bdud kyis smras pa/ gzhin bzangs dag deng la/ gal te dge slong go'u ta ma 'di gsod nus na slar shog shig/ ji ste nus na bdag cag
13b3(tog gzungs): gi gnas nas kyang bsrung gis slar shog shig/ de nas bdud kyi 'khor dkrigs phrag bcu gnyis pa de dag de nas 'phags te/ 'di nas steng du dpag tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong gi bar du
13b4(tog gzungs): bkang nas de 'dra ba'i bdud kyi stobs kyi yul gyi rdzu 'phrul drag po stan te/ gang gling bzhi pa'i nam mkha' sprin nag po chen po dang / rlung nag po chen po dang / skar mdas bkang nas
13b5(tog gzungs): ri'i rgyal po ri rab la yang lag gis gdab/ gling bzhi pa thams cad rab tu g.yo bar byas nas shin du 'jigs pa'i sgra rnams kyang 'byin te// de dag gis klu dang klu chen po
13b6(tog gzungs): dang / gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin chen po dag gis sa chen po brag dang rir bcas pa thams cad dang ldan pa dang / ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyang g.yos par rig mche dang mtsho chen
13b7(tog gzungs): po dang / 'bab chu dang chu bran dang / 'bab chu chen po dang / rgya mtsho chen po rnams kyang 'khrugs par rig nas/ nam mkha'i dkyil na 'khod do// bdud kyi 'khor de dag ni ri rab
14a1(tog gzungs): kyi 'om la 'khod nas dpagra tshad tsam gyi rdo'i char mngon par skul te/ namakha' las kun du 'beb so// ral gri dang / gtun shing dang / rdo ba dang / mtshon rtse gnyis pa
14a2(tog gzungs): dang / ste'u ka ma dang / lcags mda' dang / spu gr-i lte bu dang / dgra sta dang / ste'u so lta bu dang / ste'u so dang / kha rod can dang / kha shin du ring rod can dang / sra ba drag pa rtsub pa rno
14a3(tog gzungs): char rab tu sprul te/ kun du phang po// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das bdud kyi 'khor rnam par 'jig pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhug ste/ gang rdo ba dang
14a4(tog gzungs): mtshon cha de dag thams cad lha'i me tegre ud pa la dang / pad ma dang / pad ma dkar po dang / man d+ha ra ba dang / man d+ha ra ba chen po'i me tog gi char chen por byin gyis brlabs/ yul
14a5(tog gzungs): ang+ga mang+ga tAr skar mda' ltung ba ni spos kyi cher chen po byin gyis brlabs/ sgra de dag ni rol mo'i sgra sna tshogasu byin gyis brlabs te/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi sgra dang / chos kyi sgra dang / 
14a6(tog gzungs): dge 'dun gyi sgra dang / pha rol du phyin pa'i sgra dang / mngon par shes pa'i sgra dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sgra dang / dbang skur ba'i sgra dang / bdud bani pham par bya ba'i sgra dang / byang chub kyi snying pa la
14a7(tog gzungs): 'gro ba'i sgra dang / len pa dang bcas pa dang / len pa med pa'i bar gyi sgrar byin gyis brlab so// rdul dang mun pa nag dang rlung thams cad kyang rab tu zhi ba'o// gang kring bzhi pa 'di
14b1(tog gzungs): na rtswa dang shing gel ba dang / sman dang / nags tsha ba dang / sa dang / brag dang / ri ci yod pa de dag thams cad ni rin po che sna bdun du byin gyis brlab so// bcom ldan 'das gtsug tor mi
14b2(tog gzungs): mthong ba dang ldan pa ni tshangs pa'i 'jig rten gyi bar du sku dbang mdzad do// bcom ldan 'das kyis mtshon re re las kyang 'di 'dra ba'i 'od byung ste/ 'od des stong gsum gyi stong chen
14b3(tog gzungs): po'i 'jig rten gyi khams snang ba chen pos khyab par gyur to// stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri dang lha ma yin dang / 
14b4(tog gzungs): ninam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / yi dgas dang / sha za dang / grul bum la dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / sems can dmyal ba pa dang / dad 'gro'i skye gnas
14b5(tog gzungs): ba dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa de dag thams cad kyis/ bcom ldan 'das mthong nas lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am
14b6(tog gzungs): ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / nam mkha' la 'khod pa brgya stong mang pos ni/ me tog gtor cing bstod nas bskor ba byaso// sems can dmyal ba chen po dang
14b7(tog gzungs): dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa mi 'khrugs pa phrag bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po ni dran pa rnyed nas dge ba'i rtsa ba sngon bskyed pa dran nas// sangs rgyas la
15a1(tog gzungs): phyag 'tshalo zhes byas te ngan song de dag nas shi 'phos nas lhar skyes so// bdud kyi sde de'i nang nas bdud kyi bu nye khri tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das kyi
15a2(tog gzungs): cho 'phrul chen po 'di lta bu mthong nas/ bcom ldan 'das la rab tu dga' bar gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der dong ste phyin pa dang / bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu btso
15a3(tog gzungs): ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ thal mo sbyar nas tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// rnam dag sku lnga mchog tu gzugs bzang ba// ye shes rgya mtsho gas
15a4(tog gzungs): gyi lhun po 'dra// grags pa 'jig rten gsum na lam me ba/ mgon po khyod nyid la ni skyab su mchi/ rab tu lam stor rnam par mi bzlums la// khyed ni 'jig rten sgron ma
15a5(tog gzungs): nyi ma 'dra/ gzhan gyis mi thub srog chags rtsa lag gcig/ ded dpon khyod la skyabasu rab tu mchi// shin du tshogs bsags ye shes 'byor bar mdzod/ nam mkha'i rang
15a6(tog gzungs): bzhin bzod nas rnam grol thugs// thugs rje bsam pa yid 'ong 'jam pa'i gsung // don kun grub pa khyod la skyab su mchi// 'khor ba dgon pa las ni khyod mthar mdzad
15a7(tog gzungs): tshogs pa las kyang rgyu dang 'bras bu stoni/ byams la gnas shing mchog gi cho ga mkhyen/ thugs ji gnas pa'i skyab su mche/ sbrum smrig sku chu zla 'dra ba lo// srid pa la ni
15b1(tog gzungs): yul gyi gnas kyis chags// mi shes nad sel 'jig rten rnams kyi ma mgon/ sman pa'i rgyal po khyod la skyab su mchi// chu bo bzhi dbus zam par gyur pa khyod/ nor bdun 'jas
15b2(tog gzungs): pa'i tshul gyis rab sgrol ba/ yang dag lam ston 'jig rten rtsa lag go/ thugs rje ldan pa khyod la 'dir mchod do// blo mchog khyod la bdag cag bzod par gsol// khyod la bdag cag
15b3(tog gzungs): yid kyis gnod bsams pa// mgon po dpa' bo nongs pa bzod par gsol// khyod ni 'gro ba'i rtsa lag gcig pu gtso// bdag cag bdud kyi phyogs ni rab spangs te/ byang chub mchog
15b4(tog gzungs): gi sems ni bskyed par bgyi/ sems can ma lus thams cad 'gron du gnyer/ bdag cag gi ni byang chub mchog thob bgyi// ci nas bdag cag pha rol phyin la spyod// bdag cag rnams
15b5(tog gzungs): la spyod pa rgya cher ston// gzhan ma yin gsung chos rnams dang / ldan na byang chub rab tu thob par 'gyur// me tog gang gis khyod la mngon par gtor// phyogs kun du yang de dag
15b6(tog gzungs): gdugs gyur te/ dus kun bde ba'i 'byung gnas zhing du ni// rkang gnyis mchog gi spyi bor 'dus gyur cig/ de nas bdud kyi bu mo de dag dang / bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang
15b7(tog gzungs): bcas pa de dag thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das la me tog sil ma gtor ba dang / me tog sil ma de dag bcom ldan 'das kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus/ gang gi'i klung bye
15'a1(tog gzungs): khrag khrig brgya stong gi be ma las 'das pa'i me tog gi gdugs kun du 'dug par gyur te/ me tog gi gdugs de dag kyang phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
15'a2(tog gzungs): bzhugs shing 'tshal ba zhes pa thams cad kyi/ dbu gtsug gi drang thad kyi steng gi bair snang la 'dug go// bdud kyi bu mo de dag dang / bdud kyi tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag kya
15'a3(tog gzungs): so so nas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med dpag tu med pa thams cad na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bzhugs shing 'tshol ba zhes te/ chos kyang 'chad pa 'khor gyis
15'a4(tog gzungs): yongasu bskor te/ lham me lhan ne lhang der bzhugs pa'i dbu rtsig gi drang thad kyi bar snang la// me tog gi gdugs de dag bdug par 'gyur ba mthong zhing / sangs rgyas bcom ldan
15'a5(tog gzungs): 'das de dag kyang kha dog mtshungs pa/ rtags mtshungs pa gzugs 'dra bar mtshungs par snang ba sha stag la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag seng ge'i khri tha dad cing 'khor tha
15'a6(tog gzungs): dad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan bkod pa nyi tshe tha dad par mthong ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi gsung brjod pa ni ma thos so// bdud kyi
15'a7(tog gzungs): 'khor de dag bcom ldan 'das kyi mthus/ 'di lta bu'i cho 'phrul mthong na mchog tu dga' ba dang / mos paskyes te bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la 'go bos phyag 'tshal nas/ chos
15'b1(tog gzungs): nyan pa'i phyir spyan sngar 'khod do// de nas bdud kyi tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag las 'khris phrag bcu phyir log nas bdud kyi gan su de lta bu'i ngo mtshar bdud sdig can lnga
15'b2(tog gzungs): rgya cher bzlas te/ dge sbyong ko'u ta ma de'i sku'i khung bu gcig kyang bdag cag gis bzhig ma nus na/ bsad pa lta ci smos/ de'i steng du nyi khri de'i skyabasu dong ste// chos nyan pa'i phyir
15'b3(tog gzungs): de'i mdun du 'khod do// de nas bdud sdig can rab tu 'khros te// sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde ba nas yid la bcags te/ des 'di skad ces smras// shAkya'i bu 'di ji srid cig bklag
15'b4(tog gzungs): par ma byas/ de srid rab tu nga'i dpal song slar mi 'ong // shAkya'i bu 'di ji ltar de ring bsad snyam ste// bdag cag gzhan la yid mi rtog cing mi smra 'dug/ de nas bdud sdig can yid mi bde
15'b5(tog gzungs): zhing mya ngan gyi khang pa na 'dug go// / 'dus pa rin po che tog gi gzungs las bdud spa skong ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// / de nas bdud kyi bu mo dang bdud kyi bu
15'b6(tog gzungs): tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag ni/ 'di lta bu'i theg pa dang / ye shes dang / rdzu 'phrul dang snying
15'b7(tog gzungs): dang / thabs dang spobs pa 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / ye shes kyi bar du ldan pa ngo mtshar to// bcom ldan 'das chos dang ldan na/ skyes bu
16a1(tog gzungs): gang zag sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu mi 'chi zhing myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka
16a2(tog gzungs): bstsal pa/ rigs kyi bu dag chos bzhi dang ldan na/ 'di la skyes bu gang zag la la sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu mi 'gro zhing // myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par
16a3(tog gzungs): rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// bzhi gang zhe na/ gzhin bzangs dag 'di la rigs kyi bu chos thams cad la mchog tu mi 'dzin cing / chos gang yang mi 'dzin mi gtong / khas mi len mi gnas
16a4(tog gzungs): nye bar mi len mi rtog/ rnam par mi rtag/ 'di lta ste/ sbyin pa'i pha rol du phyin pa la spyod na/ sbyin pa'i 'bras bu yang mi rtog/ mi 'dzin khas mi len nye bar mi len/ mi gnas mi rtog rnam
16a5(tog gzungs): par mi rtog ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i bar du spyod pa na/ mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'i bar du'o// gzhin bzangs dag gzhan yang rigs kyi bu de/ sems can du smra ba ma yin/ 
16a6(tog gzungs): srog tu smra ba yin/ gso ba ma yin/ gang zag tu smra ba ma yin zhing / sems can gyi khams la yid kyis mchog tu mi 'dzin pa nas/ mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'i bar du'o// gzhin
16a7(tog gzungs): bzangs dag gzhan yang rigs kyi bu de gzugs dang / sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya las mi 'dzin pas na/ mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'i bar da'o// gzhin bzangs dag gzhan yang
16b1(tog gzungs): rigs kyi bu khams gsum dang / dus gsum tu dang phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched rnams kyi rgyu dang / rkyen dang dmigs pa dang / 'bras bu rnam par smin pa 'byung ba dang / gnas dang
16b2(tog gzungs): skye ba thams cad la mchog tu mi 'dzin pa nas mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'i bar du'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ni spyod pa'i gnas kyi yul thams cad la/ rtog
16b3(tog gzungs): pa dang / rnam par rtog pa dang bral ba ste/ mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis spyad par bya'o// gzhin bzangs dag chos thams cad dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni dngos po med pa yin te/ 
16b4(tog gzungs): sgra med pa/ mtshan ma med pa yi ge med pa/ sman pa med pa/ skye ba med pa/ 'gog pa med pa mtshan nyid med pa/ chags pa med pa/ dmigs pa med pa/ bstan du med pa/ dben pa dag
16b5(tog gzungs): med pa/ mtshan nyid dang bral ba skad cig ma nye bar zhi ba/ mun pa med pa/ snang ba med pa/ gnas med pa/ yul med pa/ dbang po med pa/ phyogs med pa/ mnyen po med pa/ bas
16b6(tog gzungs): du med pa/ mi 'phrogs pa/ ser sna med pa/ spobs pa med pa/ rdul med pa/ rdul dang bral ba/ cha shes med pa/ ci yang med pa/ byed pa po med pa/ tshor ba po med pa/ rten med
16b7(tog gzungs): bai/ gzung ba med pa/ rnam par rig pa med pa/ so sor snang ba med pa/ skad cig ma ma yin pa'i bar du'o// gzhin bzangs dag ma thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni namakhar
17a1(tog gzungs): dang mtshungs te stong pa nyid dmyig su med pa'i tshul dang / mi gnas pa'i tshul dang mchog tu 'dzin pa med pa'i tshul dang / mi rtog rnam par mi rtog pa'i tshul
17a2(tog gzungs): gyis spyad par bgyi'o// gzhin bzangs dag chos bzhi po de dag dang ldan na/ skyes bu gang zag sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu mi 'gro zhing / myur du bla na med pa yang dag par
17a3(tog gzungs): rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// gzhin bzangs dag gang la la yul thams cad la chags pa'i lus kyi mtshan nyid la rnam par spyod pas/ thams
17a4(tog gzungs): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol na/ de gnyis la chags pa yin te/ de gnyis la chags pa'i yid kyi rnam pa ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid sla bar byed do// de la gnyis gang zhe
17a5(tog gzungs): na/ gang phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la mtshan nyid du rnam par spyod pa dang / gnas pa dang mchog tu 'dzin pa de nyis ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du smra ba'o// spyod 'i
17a6(tog gzungs): gnas dang / 'bras bu la rtogs pa 'di ni gnyis so// skye ba dang / srid pa dang / len pa dang / sems can gyi gnas la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// bshad pa dang rab tu bstan pa dang / 
17a7(tog gzungs): gdams pa dang / tshig gi lam dang / sgra dang skad kyi gnas la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis// rtag pa dang chud pa la rnam par lta ba'i shes pa dang / shes par bya ba'i gnas la rtogs pa 'di
17b1(tog gzungs): ni gnyis so// sems can dang srog dang / gso pa dang / skyes pa dang gang zag dang / byed pa po dang / byed du 'jug pa po'i 'du shes kyi gnas la rtogs pa 'di ni gnyis so// gang pa
17b2(tog gzungs): rol dang / tshu rol dang / rtog pa dang sel ba la gnas shing rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// gzhin bzangs dog skyes pa gang dag su la la thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol ba de/ 
17b3(tog gzungs): dus gsum du ngar 'dzin pa dang / nga yir 'dzin pa dang / kun 'byung ba dang / 'gog pa rnam par spyod pa la gnas shing kun du rtog ste/ mchog tu 'dzin na/ 'di ni thams cad mkhye
17b4(tog gzungs): pa'i ye shes de smra ba gnyis so// 'di lta ste dper na skyes bu la la zhig/ me 'dod pa la sa'i ngos la nyug pa dang / skom 'dod pa la me dang / zas 'dod pa la rdo dang / me tog
17b5(tog gzungs): 'dod pa la gos dang / spos 'dod pa la mi ro bam pa dang / gos 'dod pa la dur khrod dang / byug pa 'dod pa la nam mkha' la myug pa de bzhin du/ gzhin bzangs dag gang spyod pa'i
17b6(tog gzungs): gnas la chags shing / rnam par spyod pa'i lus gnyis kyi gnas kyis/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol na/ de'i 'bad pa'i 'bras bu med pa yin no// de nas byang chub
17b7(tog gzungs): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mchog gi blo gros zhes bya ba 'khor der 'dus par gyur nas/ 'dug pa des bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de log su thal mo sbyar ba btud
18a1(tog gzungs): de 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gang brjod du ma mchis pa de/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar nus pa lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
18a2(tog gzungs): bstsal pa/ gang brjed du med par shes pa de nyid mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// de'i phyir rigs kyi bu khyod nyid la dris/ khyod kyis ji ltar bzod pa bzhin du lan thob cig/ gang
18a3(tog gzungs): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ming thob par 'gyur ba'i rdzas kyi dngos po gang yang yod dam/ gsol pa gal te mchis shes pa gyis na ni rtag par 'gyur// ci ste ma mchis zhes bgyis na ni chad
18a4(tog gzungs): par 'gyur to// dbu ma'i lam ni dmigasu ma mchis te/ de ni mchis par yang ma lags/ ma mchis par yang ma lag so// gang ma chags mi skye mi 'gog tshad ma mchis/ grangs ma mchis
18a5(tog gzungs): dpe ma mchis/ snang ba ma mchis pa de la 'tshal ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' klog gi blo gros kyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang la 'gro/ 
18a6(tog gzungs): ba yang ma mchis/ 'ong ba yang ma mchis pa de lta bu shes pa yang 'jug par mkhas pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ 
18a7(tog gzungs): gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang na thob pa'i mtshan nyid kyang da yin/ ma mchis ma thob pa'i mtshan nyid ma mchis mngon par rtogs par yang ma mchis/ mngon du bgyid pa la
18b1(tog gzungs): ma mchis// zhi ba yang ma mchis/ rab tu zhi ba yang ma mchis// dus gsum pa yang ma mchis/ theg pa gsum po yang ma mchis/ smon lam dang mnyam pa'i rlom sems kyang ma
18b2(tog gzungs): mchis pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi blo grospyi gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das khams gsum yang ma mchis// kun du sbyor ba
18b3(tog gzungs): gsum yang ma mchis/ rig pa gsum yang ma mchis/ theg pa gsum yang ma mchis/ phung po dang khams dang skye mched la rtogs pa yang ma mchis/ rnam par rtog pa yang ma mchis
18b4(tog gzungs): 'bri ba yang ma mchis/ 'phel ba yang ma mchis/ mnyam par yang mi bgyid pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje blo gros kyis gsol pa/ 
18b5(tog gzungs): gang so so'i skye bo'i chos dang / 'phags pa'i chos dang / slob pa'i chos dang / mi slob pa'i chos dang / nyan thos kyi chos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la mi rtog/ rnam par mi rtog ste/ 
18b6(tog gzungs): mnyam par ma bgyid pa de ni/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sra ba'i blo gros kyis gsol pa/ gang dben pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin nyid la rnam par spyod
18b7(tog gzungs): cing mngon par mi zhen pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' lag na rin po ches gsol pa/ gang chos thams cad mi skye ba'i mtshan nyid thob par bgyid
19a1(tog gzungs): pa dang / mngon par rtogs par bgyi ba'i slad du mi rtog pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros bsam gyis
19a2(tog gzungs): mi khyab pas gsol pa// khams gsum la rnam par spyod cing sems nyid sems la 'jug par bgyid de/ sems nyid sems kyi rnam par dpyad nas mi dmigs pa
19a3(tog gzungs): 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' dag las rnam par rgyal gyis gsol pa/ gang chos thams cad la mi chags rje su ma chags/ btang snyos
19a4(tog gzungs): su mi bgyid// 2khong khro bar mi bgyid/ 'dod par mi bgyid mi myong bar mi 'dzin/ mi gtong ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' pad ma'i/ 
19a5(tog gzungs): snying pos gsol pa/ gang bsod nams dang sdig pa la mi chags shing zab mo la bzod pa'i tshul la 'jug pa dang / ngar 'dzin pa dang / nga yir 'dzin pa la mi rtog pa 'di ni mngon par
19a6(tog gzungs): rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// zla 'od gzhon nur gyur pas gsol pa/ gang chos thams cad chu zla dang mtshungs par rab tu 'tshal zhing chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid la sogs pa dang 'bri/ 
19a7(tog gzungs): bar mi mthong ba bzhi ni/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros gzhon nur gyur pA/ gang gi sems dang sems las byung ba la mun pa
19b1(tog gzungs): dang / snang ba dang / skye ba dang 'jig pa dang / 'phel ba dang 'bri ba thams cad mi 'byung ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' byams pas
19b2(tog gzungs): gsol pa/ gang gnas pa la gnas pas na/ khams gsum pa la gnas pa'i tshangs pa la mi dmigs/ mnyam par mi bgyid pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
19b3(tog gzungs): rgya'o// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros mi zad pas gsol ba// gang 'khor gsum yongasu dag pas/ pha rol du phyin pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rab tu goms
19b4(tog gzungs): bar bgyid cing / mi chags mi skye ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang chos thams cad la mi
19b5(tog gzungs): chags mi skyo zhing zab mo'i tshul yang rab tu 'tshal ba de yang mi len mi 'dar ba/ sdud par mi bgyid 'bral bar mi bgyid cing chos gang la yang spyod pa 'am/ bri ba 'am/ rig
19b6(tog gzungs): pa 'am/ rnam par grol ba'am/ 'jig pa'am/ bri ba 'am/ 'phel ba yang mi skye la/ dngos po dag la rnam par mi rtog pas/ kun nas nyon mongs par yang mi 'gyur ba 'di
19b7(tog gzungs): ni/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ste/ tshul cig po 'dis thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ltad mo can
20a1(tog gzungs): gyis smras pa/ 'jam dpal de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa'i tshul/ ji ltar zab mo stong pa nyid sgom pa'i tshul 'di gcig gis/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mngon par
20a2(tog gzungs): rdzogs par 'tshang rgyan/ kan sbyor ba dang rab tu sbyor ba ci dgos// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ lta ba mi zad pa dang bral zhing yang dag par lta bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / g.yo
20a3(tog gzungs): med cing drang por sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / sdig pa yang bral zhing bla ma la ri mor bya bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / bka' blo bde bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / yang
20a4(tog gzungs): dag 'tsho bar sgro 'dogs pa dang / kun sbyor ba thams cad dang bral bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / sems can thams cad la 'khro ba dang snying rje bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa
20a5(tog gzungs): sdom pa gsum du sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / mi slu ba dge ba'i chos su sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / rnam par ma zhi bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / dam pa'i chos
20a6(tog gzungs): srung bar sgro 'dogs pa yong med pa dang / sems can thams cad yongasu mi gtong bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / dngos po thams cad yongasu gtong bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med
20a7(tog gzungs): pa dang / sems can nyams chung ba stobs la rab tu dgod par sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / 'jigs pa'i skyabs mi 'jigs par yang sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / lam ngan par/ 
20b1(tog gzungs): zhugs pa rnams nan tan la bzung bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / bzod pa dang nges par sgro 'dogs pa med pa dang / 'dzin pa thams cad la chags pa'i mtshan nyid du sgro 'dog
20b2(tog gzungs): pa yang med pa dang / brdul dang mun pa'i phung po thams cad spong bar sgro 'dogs pa yang med pa dang / bsngo ba'i 'bras bu rnam par smin pa thams cad spong bar sgro 'dogs parwa yang med pa
20b3(tog gzungs): 'di dag thams cad ni/ rigs kyi bu thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sbyor ba nyi shu ste/ yi ge dang / skad dang / smra ba dang brjod pa'i tshig tu dbye ba thams cad kyi de bzhin la 'jug pa'i
20b4(tog gzungs): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sbyor ba'o// gzhan mu stegs can gyi tshig gi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa dang / spyod pa thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa dang / bsod nams
20b5(tog gzungs): thams cad dang de bzhin nyi shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa la sbyar ba'i de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa dang / len pa dang / skye ba dang / 'jigs pa thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug
20b6(tog gzungs): pa dang / rnam par thar pa gsum dang / gnas dang / rgyu dang / las dang / chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' thams cad shes nus/ thams cad
20b7(tog gzungs): mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sbyor ba khong du chud par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' ltad mo can gyis smras pa/ 'jam dpal de de bzhin te/ nam chos zab mo'i tshul 'di rtogs pa
21a1(tog gzungs): de'i tshe chos gang bstan pa dang / gang la ston pa dang / don dang tshig dang / yi ge gang dag gis ston pa dang / rab tu ston pa'i chos gang yang mi mthong ste/ gang rab tu
21a2(tog gzungs): spong ba dang / gang sgom pa dang / gang kun shes par 'gyur ba'i chos thams cad brjod du med pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin nyid la 'jug ste/ des thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes khong du
21a3(tog gzungs): chud par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ leg so legaso/ rigs kyi bu tshul cig gis thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes thob pa de/ khyod kyis legs par smras so// de
21a4(tog gzungs): ci'i phyir zhe na/ thams cad la chags pa med pa'i dngos po yin pas/ chos thams cad ni sgro btags pa med pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / mi 'jigs pa'i mtha' can dang / ma rig pa dang / mya
21a5(tog gzungs): ngan las 'das pa'i mi skye ba'i yang dag pa'i mtha' can dang / nam mkha' dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha' can dang / chos thams cad ni brjod du med pa'i mtha' can dang // 
21a6(tog gzungs): sems can thams cad kyang de lta bu yin pa dang / chos thams cad ni rdzas med pa'i mtha' can dang / dus gsum dang / khams gsum thams cad ni ci yang med pa'i mtha' can dang / 'du
21a7(tog gzungs): byed gsum ni stong pa nyid kyi mtha' dang / chos kyi phung po dang / rnam par smin pa'i phung po dang / sogs pa dang bri ba'i phung po ni rdzas med pa'i mtha' can du yongasu brjod do// stong pa nyid
21b1(tog gzungs): dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' dang / brjod du med pa'i don dang / chos thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la
21b2(tog gzungs): 'jug go/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes thob pa/ lung bstan pa 'di bshad pa'i tshe/ bdud kyi bu mi dang / bdud kyi bu'i tshogs kyi 'khor nyi khris/ mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob
21b3(tog gzungs): ste/ lus rags pa spangs nas yid kyi lus rnyed de/ gzhan nyi khri brgyad stong gis ni mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par gyur to// lha dang mi dkrugs phrag dgu bcu rtsa gnyis kyis ni
21b4(tog gzungs): byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa dang / ting 'dzin dang / gzugs sna tshogs thob par gyur te/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pa nyi khri
21b5(tog gzungs): po de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la lha'i me tog gis gtor rab tu gter nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te// 'di skad ces gsol te/ bcom ldan
21b6(tog gzungs): 'das 'di ltar mi dge ba'i grogs po dang / grogs po'i dbang gis sems can rnams ye bsod nams thams cad la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yid la mi bgyid pa la gzigs
21b7(tog gzungs): gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ de ni las kyi rkyen yin par lta'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis the/ ngo mtshar du gyur pa'i sems can rnams kyi the tsom
22a1(tog gzungs): bcad pa'i phyir/ sngon 'byung ba 'di gsungaso// rigs kyi bu sngon 'byung ba 'das pa'i dus skal pa chen po dpag tu med pa 'das pa de'i tshe de'i dus na gling bzhi pa'i 'jig
22a2(tog gzungs): rten gyi khams 'di nyid du snang ba 'chang ba zhes bya ba'i bskal pa chen po la skye rgu'i tshe lo drug khri brgyad stong thub ste/ de'i tshe de'i dus na de bzhin gshegs pa 'od bzhi spos snang
22a3(tog gzungs): dpal zhes bya ba rig pa dang zhab su ldan pa// bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo bsgyur ba bla na med pa lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs
22a4(tog gzungs): rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'byung ste/ nyon mongs pa can snyigs ma lnga'i dus su gyur pa na/ 'khor bzhi la theg pa gsum dang ldan pa'i chos ston to// yang de'i tshe gling bzhi la dbang
22a5(tog gzungs): ba'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong zhes bya ba gcig byung ste/ de nas 'dus gzhan zhig gi tshe/ rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong btsun mo'i 'khor dang g.yog dang dpung
22a6(tog gzungs): gi tshogs dang bcas te de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi smros snang dpal ga la ba der dong nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal to// bcom ldan 'dra
22a7(tog gzungs): la me tog sna tshogs kyis gtor cig/ sil snyan sna tshogs dang / bdug pa sna tshogs dang / spos sna tshogs kyis mchod pa byas nas// lan gsum skor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan
22b1(tog gzungs): 'das dge slong gi dge 'dun du bcas pa'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas// tshig su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// lha dang klu la sogs pa yon tan gyis mngon
22b2(tog gzungs): par rab sted nyes pa mang sol dang // nor bdun gyis ni 'gro la phan mdzad pa// gang gis blo gros zhi dang ldan 'gyur gsungs// 'gro ba'i mun sol zhi ba sgron mdzad pa// shi 'phon/ 
22b3(tog gzungs): mchi skye ba mya ngan 'jom// 'gro ba ngan song gsum las rab sgrol ba// gang gis bdud kyi lam las thar gsungs// rigs kyi bu de nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'od ni spros snang dpal
22b4(tog gzungs): des// rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong de la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// skyes bu dam pa chos gsum dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' blo gros zhi ba yin te gsu mi gang zhe na// 
22b5(tog gzungs): 'di lta ste/ lhag pa'i bsam pas sems can thams cad la snying rje ba dang / ma lta bur sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar bya ba la brtson pa dang / chos thams cad la
22b6(tog gzungs): srog med pa dang / gso ba med pa dang / gang zag med pa dang / tha dad du dbyer med cing mnyam par yongs su rtog pa ste/ skyes bu dam pa chos gsum po de dag dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa'
22b7(tog gzungs): blo gros zhi ba yin te/ rgyal po chen po gzhan yang chos gsum dang ldan na/ skyes bu dam pa bdud kyi zhags pas mi 'dzin cing bdud kyi lam las thar te gsum gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 
23a1(tog gzungs): sems can thams cad la mi khro zhing klan ka mi tshol ba yin sems can thams cad la mtshungs par sbyin gan su shes pa yin/ chos thams cad la tshul cig tu yongasu rtog skye
23a2(tog gzungs): 'di ltar chos thams cad nam mkha' dang mtshungs shing bcosu med pa ma yin pa/ ma skyes pa ma byung ba/ ma 'gags pa ste/ chos thams cad nam mkha' lta bu rdzas kyis/ mtshan nyid
23a3(tog gzungs): dang bral bar mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rab tu rtog pa'o// rgyal po chen po chos gsum po de dang ldan na/ skyes bu dam pa bdud kyi zhags pas ma zin cing / bdud kyi lam las thar te/ 
23a4(tog gzungs): ba yin no// de nas de'i tshe rgyal po chen po ud pa la'i gdong gi btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes zhes bya ba bud med brgyad khri bzhi stong gis yongasu brdar nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
23a5(tog gzungs): 'od zhi spos snang dpal la me tog sna tshogs kyis gtor te/ tshig su bcad pa 'di dag gsol to// mi mnyam yon tan 'dzin pa rab rib med pa// ji ltar bud med las ni ngan song spangs pa
23a6(tog gzungs): yi// skyes par 'dir 'gyur 'chi 'pho gsal bar bka' stsol cig/ rab mchog phan pa mdzad pa myur du yid kyang 'thul// dam pa'i 'gro bzhud bde gshegs rab zhi dga' mdzad

23b1(tog gzungs): 'jig rten dag na mi mnyam mnyam pa dge mchog/ rab grags yon tan mang po dran dang 'dul ba 'dzin// ci nas 'di nyid du ni skyes pa dga' 'gyur ba// rab rib mi mnga' bde 'gro ma ni
23b2(tog gzungs): med lam du gsungs// rigs kyi bu des de skad ces gsol ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'od bzhi smos snang des/ btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// 
23b3(tog gzungs): che zhe rnam grangs gang gis bud med dag/ bud med kyi dngos po myur du rjes te/ sngon gyi 'phags pa'i bud med kyi dngos po myur du ma lus par zad par 'gyur zhing / bla na med pa'i
23b4(tog gzungs): mya ngan 'das pa chen po'i ba ra da/ rang gi smon lam ma gtogs par bud med du skye bar 'dzin par mi 'gyur ba'i rnam grangs yod do// che zhe de la rnam grangs gang gis/ bud med
23b5(tog gzungs): myur du skyes par 'gyur zhing sngon 'phags pa'i bud med kyi dngos po myur du ma lus par 'gyur ba'i rnam grangs de gang zhe na/ che zhe de la rin po che tog ces bya ba'i gzungs// rdzu 'phrul/ 
23b6(tog gzungs): chen po phan yon chen mo mthu chen mo 'di lta ste/ bud med kyi dngos po thams cad zad par byed cing // lus dang drag dang / sems kyi gnas len gyi sdug bsngal rnam par smin pa
23b7(tog gzungs): ma lus par zad par byed do// rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di thos ma thag tu bud med rnams kyis bud med kyi dngos por ma gyur te/ bud med kyi dngos po mi snang zhing / skyes
24a1(tog gzungs): ga pa'i dbang po skye bar 'gyur/ skyes pa gzugs bzang po yan lag thams cad tshang bar 'gyur/ drang zhing zhib pa shes pa la mkhas par 'gyur// lus dang ngag dang yid
24a2(tog gzungs): kyis legs par byas pa'i las kyi mtha' dang ldan pa/ legs par spyad pa spyod pa dang / dgra thams cad thul bar 'gyur ro// gang gi tshe 'di dang tshe rabs phyi ma la/ las dang ngag dang yid
24a3(tog gzungs): kyi sdug bsngal ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i nyes pa byas pa'i las kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa de yongasu zad par 'gyur te/ 'tshams med pa byed pa dang / dam pa'i chos spong ba dang
24a4(tog gzungs): 'phags pa la skur pa 'debs pa dag ma rtogs par de dag gi bud med kyi dngos po'i lhag ma ma lus pa tshe de nyid la yongasu zad par 'gyur ro// lus dang ngag dang yid kyi nga gnas ngan
24a5(tog gzungs): len gyi/ rnam par smin pa de gzhan la bud med kyi dngos po grub par byed pa'i sa bon sdug bsngal rnam par smin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i las kyi sgrib pa'i sa bon gyi rgyu 'thun pa'i
24a6(tog gzungs): ri rab tsam yang ma lus par yongasu zad par 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal gyi rnam par smin pa'i las yongasu zad par bya ba dang
24a7(tog gzungs): dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par spel ba'i phyir/ 'das pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang / rin po che tog gi gzungs
24b1(tog gzungs): bshad de/ byin gyis brlab so// cig la gcig rjes dge so/ mngon par bstod do// bsdogaso/ rab tu bsngags so// de ltar phyogs bcu na da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa
24b2(tog gzungs): dgra bcom pa yang dag par zhugs te/ 'tsho zhing bzhes pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag thams cad kyang rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing dag na/ sems can rnams kyi nyes
24b3(tog gzungs): par byas pa'i las yongasasu zad par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par spel bar bya ba'i phyir rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di 'chad de/ rab tu sngags pa'i bar du mdzad do// gang dag ma 'ong
24b4(tog gzungs): pa'i dus na/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing so sor 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag kyang sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal
24b5(tog gzungs): rnam par smin pa de yongasu zad par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par spel ba'i phyir// rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di 'chad pa rnams la yang rje 'gyur te/ rab tu bsngags pa'i bar
24b6(tog gzungs): mdzad par 'gyuraro// da ltar nga yang rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di 'chad de/ phyogs bcu na da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di 'chad pa rnams
24b7(tog gzungs): la yang rjes su yid rang ngo // bsngagaso rab tu ston to// che zhe rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba skye bo'i nang nas mthu dang dbang thob pa gang la las rin po che tog gi/ 
25a1(tog gzungs): gzungs 'di glegs bam du bris te 'chang na rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bos dbang bskur ba de'i sran pa dang / skra dang tshigasu bcad pa phyogs bcu rgya cher grags par 'gyur te/ 
25a2(tog gzungs): gzugs kyi khams thams cad kyi bar du sgra dang / tshig snyan ga rgya chen pos gang bar 'gyur ro// lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci
25a3(tog gzungs): bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma rgyal rigs spyi bos dbang bskur ba de/ bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang / sra bo'i phyir phyi bzhin 'brang zhing gnaso// de'i yul thams cad du 'thab mo dang / 
25a4(tog gzungs): brtsod pa dang / mu ge dang / nad dang pha rol gyi dmag tshogs dang / dus ma yin dang / tshar dang / grang ba dang / tsha ba'i nyes pa rab tu zhi bar 'gyu ro// gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang / seng ge dang / 
25a5(tog gzungs): ma he dang / glang po che dang / spyang khyim rungs pa thams cad kyang gnod par mi 'gyur/ dug dang kha ba dang / tsha ba dang / sgyu ma med pa dang / ro med pa dang / rtsub pa'i sdug bsngal ba dang / reg na
25a6(tog gzungs): mi bde bar 'gyur ba'i nyes pa thams cad kyang rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// nor dang 'bru dang / sman dang / 'bras bu dang / 'dab ma dang / me tog thams cad rab tu skye zhing rnam par 'phel/ 
25a7(tog gzungs): te/ snum pa dang ro nim par 'gyur ro// gal te rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba/ g.yul du nye bar gnas pa'i tshe// rin po che tog gzungs 'di'i glegs ba ma 'am
25b1(tog gzungs): rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo la thogs te/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba des// pha rol gyi dmag tshogs thub par 'gyur ro// de'i tshe rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang skur ba
25b2(tog gzungs): des/ pha rol gyi dmag gi dpung dang / g.yul du zhugs pa gnyi ka/ rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di'i glegs bam/ rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo la thogs te/ de gnyis gcig la cig dga'
25b3(tog gzungs): zhing 'thun par 'gyur ro// de ltar rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di yon tan dang / phan yon mang po grong ngam grong khyer ram/ grong brdal lam mi 'am rkang bzhi pa dag na 'am/ dus ma yin
25b4(tog gzungs): par 'chi ba 'am/ gnod pa zhig byung na der rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di glegs bam la mchod pa'i phyir rgya cher byas te bzhag la/ shin du khrus byas shing lus rab tu byugs shing
25b5(tog gzungs): gos sar pa bgos te tshangs par spyad de/ sing ge'i khri me tog sna tshogs kyis gtor ba/ dri sna tshogs kyis gdugs pa/ ro bro ba sna tshogs kyis bskor ba la 'dug pa la/ der rin po che tog gi gzungs
25b6(tog gzungs): 'di glegs bam la bklags na/ der nad dang / ngas ma yin par 'chi ba thams cad rab tu zhi bar 'gyuraro// des 'jigs shing spu zing zhes byed pa dang / ltas ngan pa thams cad med par
25b7(tog gzungs): 'gyur ro// bud med gang la la/ bu 'dod na des khrus byas te/ gos gsar pa bgoso// tshangs par spyad de/ me tog dang / phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pas glegs bam de mchod la/ 
26a1(tog gzungs): bdag nyid kyang me tog sna tshogs kyis gtor ba/ dri sna tshogs kyis gdugs pa// 'bro ba sna tshogs kyis bskor ba la 'dug nas/ rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di klags na des
26a2(tog gzungs): bu rnyed par 'gyur ro/ de bla na med pa'i yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa'i bar du sems smin par bya ba'i phyir// rang gi smon lam ma rtogs par de nyid de'i bud med du 'gyur ba'i thams
26a3(tog gzungs): yin no// che zhe rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di las tha na tshig su bcad pa cig tsam/ gang la la'i rna lam du grags na ri dgas dang / bya yang rung ste de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag
26a4(tog gzungs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu dag de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa 'od bzhi spos snang dpal gyis// zhabs g.yas pa'i mthe bong la reg par mdzad
26a5(tog gzungs): de/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas kyang de'i tshe// sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir sa chen po rnam pa drug du g.yos par byin gyis brlabs nas/ phyogs bcu dag gi lha dang klu dang / gnod
26a6(tog gzungs): sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / ma~M 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / yi dgas dang / shi za dang / grul dum dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa grangs med dpag
26a7(tog gzungs): tu med pa rnams shin du skrag pa skyes par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing mi mjed 'di thams cad snang bas rgya cher khyab par gyur te/ lag 'brel lta bur mnyam par 'dug cing / de'i
26b1(tog gzungs): na ri dang shing dang rtsig pa dang / ri rab dang / khor yug dang / khor yug chen pos skrag pa skyes par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyi mthus phyogs bzhir bltas pa dang / de dag thams
26b2(tog gzungs): cad kyis mda' rgyang gang tsam na/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa mngon par mthong nas/ de dag ngo mtshar du gyur te/ thal mo sbyar nas de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de
26b3(tog gzungs): la nga lta'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa des 'di skad ces bka' bsngal to// rigs kyi bu dag gi tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'od bzhi spros
26b4(tog gzungs): snang dpal gyi zhabs g.yas pa'i mthe bong sa la reg pa yang 'di bzhin du de'i tshes g.yos par gyur/ de'i tshe 'di bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di yang lag mthil bzhin du
26b5(tog gzungs): mnyam par 'dug pa 'di bzhin du snang ba dang sa g.yos pas skrag pa skyes te/ lha dang / ku dang / lha ma yin thams cad phyogs bzhir blta zhing mda' rgyang ca gang tsam na/ 
26b6(tog gzungs): bzhin gshegs pa 'od ni spos sdang dpal de mthong nas thal mo sbyar te rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa 'od ni spos snang dpal des/ rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di gsungs
26b7(tog gzungs): 'di lta ste dz+wa lo kye/ dza l-i dza la dza la ni/ dza la pra ti/ dza hi li/ bar bu ru/ sha lag ga sha'i nam ru ho a ma me/ ba ma me ba mai/ nab men ha me/ dza ha me/ khA ba ra mAM ba ra me/ ba bA be ba
27a1(tog gzungs): ga bA be/ ba ha bI/ bang ga pe ba dza ge bA na te/ ba ra bar she/ dza la me kha/ a lA dza/ hi li/ dzan du lI/ dzan du mu khI/ ba ha ra ba ha ra/ sin d+ha pra te/ nan ti lA/ nan de
27a2(tog gzungs): na d+ha ga/ su rA yA bi ta kha tsan d+ha bi ta ga tsag shur d+yo ti shi bi ta kha/ sar+b+bakA ya/ sItA su ra bi h+ya ka/ dza kha ga dza khaM ga/ su ra kha~M gr-i/ byi ha ma/ a mri kha/ a mr-i kha/ a mr-i Sha
27a3(tog gzungs): mr-i kha/ a mr-i kha a mri khra/ a mr-i khaM am+bi kha/ a mr-i kha/ a mr-i kha/ a mr-i kha/ a m+bi kha mri kham+bi kha/ mr-i kha/ bya ba tsi da/ dkar mi/ du nA da ne/ ud da / dad+ya
27a4(tog gzungs): ya tse de gnyan/ kri da a nud bA daM/ kha ga ne ru ka/ ang gu le/ b+h+r-i gu le/ bi ba gu le/ ku la he/ in pa ri bi ba ha/ byA ba tse dag rbe/ tsa pra ta tsi pra ti/ u ma ha/ dar
27a5(tog gzungs): sha ne pa ri brta b+ha shu/ khag si ma kri ma dz+yo hi/ dzi ha dz+yo ti ni kra/ b+hai sa ra b+hi saM ra/ b+hi ra dze/ mA kr-i gra ma/ b+hi ba kri ma ma hA kr-i pa/ hi li hi li le/ ha ru na pra d+he/ sa ma ya
27a6(tog gzungs): ne khI/ dam dam/ d+hA na a prar mi shau/ pa la kun ta la/ ba khe ni par rta/ a sI b+ha ba karma khA ya/ pr-i dur b+ha ba ru sha ta ma/ a sa ma sa ma/ sa ma~M ya b+hi b+hi de na Ta thA ga
27a7(tog gzungs): swatwa/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya sgrib pas/ rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di bri shad pab zag tu sa yang tshar g.yos so// bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya tsamad
27b1(tog gzungs): kyang rin po me tog gi gzungs 'di thos ma thag tu/ mo mtshan mi snang bar gyur te/ pho maman skyes so// lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lA ma yin dang / nam
27b2(tog gzungs): mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / yi dgas dang sha za dang / grul bum dag gi bu mo grangs med dpag tu med pa rnams kyang / rin po che tog gi gzungs
27b3(tog gzungs): 'di thos ma thag tu// mo mtshan mi snang bar gyur te/ pho mtshan skyes nas de dag thams cad kyang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur te
27b4(tog gzungs): thams cad ma 'ongs pa na/ bud med kyi dngos po thob par 'gyur ba'i las kyi sgrib pa ma lus par byas nas/ bud med de dag thams cad kyis thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa
27b5(tog gzungs): shAkya thub pa de la phyag 'tshal zhing / skad chen por 'di skad ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa ngo mtshar mdzad
27b6(tog gzungs): pal phyag 'tsha'o// phyag 'tshal lo// thugs rje chen po gang gis/ bdag cag da ltar bud med kyi dngos po mi 'da' bar gyur cing / rnam pa thams cad rdzogs pa'i skyes pa'i dngos
27b7(tog gzungs): ra gyur ba sngon byung ba 'di ltar rgya cher bshad du gsol/ de lta bu'i ngo mtshar dang / tshe'i grus dang / skyobs bdag cag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems dbyed
28a1(tog gzungs): par bgyi'o/ bcom ldan 'das ston 'byung ba 'di lha dang mi dpag tu med pa rnams dbang du gyur par bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin pa
28a2(tog gzungs): pa shAkya thub pas sngon 'byung ba 'di bshad pa/ gzhin bzangs gang gi tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhe spos snang dpal gyi thad nas/ rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong gi rdzun
28a3(tog gzungs): mo lha mdzes/ bud med brgyad khri bzhi stong dang bcas pas rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di thos te/ thos ma thag tu btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes dang / bud med brgyad khri ba ni stong gi
28a4(tog gzungs): dri dgra mo mtshan mi snang bar gyur nas/ pho mtshan pa skyes pa de'i tshe/ de bzhin du lha'i bu mo nas mi'i bu mo'i bar du grangs med dpag tu med pa dag/ rin po che tog gi gzungs las
28a5(tog gzungs): thos mo thag tu/ bud med kyi dbang po mi snang bar gyur nas skyes pa'i dbang po skyes te/ bud med de dag thams cad ma 'ongs pa na/ bud med kyi dngos po thob par 'gyur ba'i las kyi
28a6(tog gzungs): sgrib bya ma lus par byang ngo // gang gi tshe rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong gi btsun mo dam pa lta mdzes btsun mo'i 'khor dang bcas pa phor gyur pa'i tshe// rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong des
28a7(tog gzungs): bu thu bo gling ba ni la dbang ba'i 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po'i dbang bskur bas dbang bskur te/ bu stong du gcig gis ma tshang ba dang / skyes bu dam pa lha mdzes dang bcas/ 
28b1(tog gzungs): mdzes kyang skyes bu dam pa brgyad khri bzhi stong dang bcas/ gzhan yang srog chags dgu khri bzhi stong dang bcas to// khyim nas byung nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'ong bzhi
28b2(tog gzungs): sram snang dpal de'i thad du sgra dang kha spu bregs gos ngur sreg bgros te/ yang dag par dad pas khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung ngo // rab tu byung nas kha don la
28b3(tog gzungs): dga' zhing tshul bzhin du yid la byed pa la brtson par gyur to// de nas de na srog chags bye ba mang po 'di snyam du sems te/ ci'o 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rab tu
28b4(tog gzungs): byung snyam nas/ de dag phan tshun 'di skad smra'o// dge sbyong 'di ni bdud kyi las la brtson pa ste/ g.yon can sgyu ma bdud kyi las dang ldan pas/ bdud kyi chos
28b5(tog gzungs): di stan cing/ la la ni pho mtshan med par byas/ la la ni ma mtshan med par byas/ la la ni skra dang kha spu glegs/ la l-i na~M gos mtshon can bskon// la la ni gos
28b6(tog gzungs): dkar po ston/ la la ni ltar skye bar chos ston/ la la ni mir skye bar/ la la ni dud 'gro'i skye gan su skye bas la la ni yi dag su skye bar/ ma la ni sems can dmyal
28b7(tog gzungs): bar skye bar/ la la ni shi 'pho ba dang / skye ba med par bya ba ro chos ston to// 'dud kyi las kyi lam la brtson shing / bud med sbyar ba'i rgyu dang ldan pa/ dge
29a1(tog gzungs): sbyong 'od zhi spos snang dpal de dge sbyong gi gzugs kyis rab tu slu ba yin gyis/ bdag cag 'di nas dong ste/ de'i gzugs dang / rtags dang / 
29a2(tog gzungs): 'dzin pa yang mi mthong ba dang / de'i tshig kyang cung zad kyang mi thos par 'dong ngo // de nas de nyid na shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul zhes bya ba zhig yod pa des tshig 'di skad
29a3(tog gzungs): ces smras so// kho bo'i chung mas dang / g.yog mo dang / bu mo gang yin pa de dag kyang dge sbyong ma rungs pa 'dis/ mo mtshan med par byas te/ skye ba'i dbang por sprul
29a4(tog gzungs): nas/ thams cad kyi 'go bregs te/ gos mtshan can bsnyen nas/ kho bo gcig pu mya ngan gyis non te/ thar nas bdag cag thams cad 'dus pa la/ gang du dge sbyong ma
29a5(tog gzungs): rungs pa/ dge sbyong sgyu ma bdud kyi zhags pa la brtson pa 'di'i sgra dang skad kyang mthos ni/ mthong ba lta smos kyang ci dgos pa'i ni khrod namang bar 'dong gis/ tshur shig
29a6(tog gzungs): kyis bya ba dang / de dag thams cad dga' ste/ de de bzhin no zhes zer ro// de nas shor ba gnon nu'i tshul dang / the tsom du gyur pa'i srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgyad stong dang / 
29a7(tog gzungs): lhan cig tu de nas dong ste yul mtha' 'khob ri khrod nyamang bar/ drang srong gi cha byad kyis skyed pa spyod cing / sems can de dag la 'di skad ces chos ston to// 'khor
29b1(tog gzungs): las thar pa yang med/ legs par byas pa dang / nyes par byas pa'i las kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa yang med na/ des chad par smra ba'i dge sbyong bdud kyi las la
29b2(tog gzungs): brtson pa zhig byung gis/ gang gis de la lta ba'i phyir 'gro ba dang / gang dag gus par smra ba dang / gang dag de'i chos nyan pa de dag sems g.yengs pa yin te/ de dag
29b3(tog gzungs): mgo dregs khyim nas byung / gos tshon can bskon dur khrod du spyad pa spyod du bcug/ slongs mo pa'i spyad pa la 'dzud/ zan za cig par byed pa lta ba mi zad pa'i yid dang
29b4(tog gzungs): ldan pa dang / rtag tu yid byung bar byed/ dben pa la gnas par dga' ba dang / granas khang du bcug 'dod pa'i dga' ba klu gar dang / phreng ba dang / dri dang / 
29b5(tog gzungs): byug pa dang / brgyan dang / lhab lbu ba dang / 'khrig pa'i chos dang / chang dang / ra re bar 'gyur ba'i btung ba spangs shing / smra ba nyung bar byed de/ de lta bur
29b6(tog gzungs): dge sbyong gi gzugs kyis chad par smra ba/ bdud kyi las la brtson pa/ de sems can rnams kyi sgrar gyur pa/ zhig byung ste/ dge sbyong go'u ta ma de'i byed pa ni
29b7(tog gzungs): mthos ma mthong ba yin par kho bos rtog so zhes/ des srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po de lta bu'i sdig pa can gyi lta ba 'dzin du 'jug go// den
31a1(tog gzungs): la rnam par rtse'o// de nas phyis btsal nas kyang gzhon nu brtsed mo byed pa dang / bzo'i las kyi mtha' dang klog cing 'dug pa dang / dga' ba'i rtsed mo'i phyir/ btsun
31a2(tog gzungs): mo'i 'khor gyi nang du song ba nas/ byang chub kyi shing drung du byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du skrag par bya'o// byang chub thob nas stan pa zhig par bya'o// zhes smon lam btab bo// de
31a3(tog gzungs): nas dge sbyong chen po ud pa la'i gdang gi shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul gyis/ smon lamo de ltar brtul te btab pa la mthu chen po dang / 'bad pa drag pos dad par byas te/ sdig pa'i gro lta ba
31a4(tog gzungs): thibs pa de las bzlog nas/ nyes pa bshags nas bcug ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed du bcug go/ de nas sher ba gzhan nu'i tshul rab tu btul
31a5(tog gzungs): zhing dad pa skyes nas/ 'di skad du snying rje chen po dang ldan pa khyod gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa de'i tshe/ byang chub thob
31a6(tog gzungs): thob nas/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan du gsol// zhes smon lam btab po// gzhin bzangs dag de'i tshe/ de'i dus na gang gis de bzhin gshegs
31a7(tog gzungs): pa 'od gzhi spos snang dpal de 'khor dang bcas pa la mchod pa dang / rim gro rnam pa du ma byas nas sreg chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong dang bcas te/ mngon par byung rab tu byung zhing
31b1(tog gzungs): srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma ni/ sdig pa'i lta bar song ba las bzlog ste/ theg pa gsum la bkod/ sems can dpag tu med pa ni 'bras bu la bkod// bud med bye ba khrag khrig
31b2(tog gzungs): brgya stong tshad med pa ni skyes pa thob par byas pa'i/ rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong zhes bya bar gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin snyam du khyod the tsom 'am/ yid gnyis sam/ som nyi za bar gyur
31b3(tog gzungs): na de ltar mi lta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nga de'i tshe de'i dus na gling bzhi la dbang ba'i 'khor lo'i bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong zhes bya bar gyur te/ ngas de lta bu'i skyes bu'i mthu
31b4(tog gzungs): byas so// gzhin bzangs dag de'i tshe de'i dus na gling btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes zhes bya ba gang gis dge sbyong thob par gyur pa de/ gzhan zhig yin snyam du khyed the tsom+b+ha yid gnyis sam
31b5(tog gzungs): som nyi za blar gyur pa de ltar mi lta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa de'i tshe de'i dus na/ btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes zhes bya bar gyur to// 
31b6(tog gzungs): gzhin bzangs de'i tshe de'i dus na/ the tsom gyur pa'i srog chags bye ba mang po dang bcas te/ sangs rgyas la mi snyan pa'i bor du zer ba shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul zhes bya ba gzhan
31b7(tog gzungs): yin snyam du khyod the tsom 'am// yid gnyis sam som nyi za bar gyur na/ de de ltar mi lta'o/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdud sdig can 'di nyid de'i tshe de'i dus ni/ shes rab gzhon nu'i
32a1(tog gzungs): tshul zhes bya bar gyur te/ gang de'i tshe ngas de'i 'khor rab tu byung bas/ de'i phyir nga la sems rab tu 'khro ba bskyed nas/ phyis smon lam btab ste/ khyod nam bla
32a2(tog gzungs): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa de'i tshe/ khyod kyis bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung stan cig ces
32a3(tog gzungs): byas so// rigs kyi bu dag khyed kyis kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od gzhi spos snang dpal de la/ ma dad cing ma sngams pa'i tshig smras so// sdig pa'i lta bar
32a4(tog gzungs): song ba bzung nas/ ngas khyod sdig pa'i lta bar song ba de las kun thar bar byas te/ rab tu byung bas de tshun chad khyed kyis sangs rgyas stong mang po la bsnyen bkur byas te// 
32a5(tog gzungs): dag la mchid pa dang / de dag la chos nyan te/ smon lam btab nas/ pha rol du phyin pa drug la spyad do// khyed lus dang ngag dang yid kyis nges par spyad pa'i las de dang / sngon skal
32a6(tog gzungs): pad mar ngan song gsum du sdug bsngal myong ngo // las kyi sgrib pa de nyid kyis da ltar bdud sdig can gyi gnas su skyes so// rin po che tog gi gzungs sngon 'byung ba'i le'u 'di
32a7(tog gzungs): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas bshad pa na/ bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya tsam de dag bud med kyi dngos po mi snang bar gyur nas/ skyes pa'i dngos por 'gyur
32b1(tog gzungs): te/ mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob po// lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i skye dgu'i sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med dpag tu med pa dag gis ni/ 
32b2(tog gzungs): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// de bzhin du sems can
32b3(tog gzungs): bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa dag ni/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// lha dang mi'i bu mo grangs med dpag tu med pa de dag
32b4(tog gzungs): ni/ bud med kyi dngos po las gyur to// skyes pa'i dngos po snyed do// 'dus pa rin po che tog gi gzungs las/ sngon 'byung ba'i le'u zhes bya ba gnyis pa'o// de na rin po
32b5(tog gzungs): gi gzungs 'di/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas bshad pa de'i tshe/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams me mjed 'di rgya cher snang bas khyab par gyur te/ sangs

46b1(tog gzungs): mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir 'khod do// de nas bdud sdig can gyis gang gi tshe/ bdud de dag thams cad g.yog dang bcas te/ dge sbyong ko'u ta ma la skyabasu
46b2(tog gzungs): dong bar mthong ba de'i tshe/ rab tu 'khrugs te skrag cing myos nas rab tu ngu zhing 'di skad ces smraso// bdag la phyin chad grogs med de/ bdag gi dpal deng thams cad stor/ bdag
46b3(tog gzungs): ni bdud kyi las las 'khyams// brtson 'grus thams brtsam par bya// bdag gi pad+ma ma rtsa nas bcad// pad ma bcad dang kun 'khrug de/ de nas sems can phyogs phyogs 'gro// 
46b4(tog gzungs): de ni tha ma'i stobs yin no// bdud sdig can gyis de ltar bsams nas/ rlung lta bar nam mkha' lwa babs nas/ srang gi pad ma go la ba der phyin nas/ pad ma de'i sdong po bcad

46b6(tog gzungs): na klag snang yang mi dmigs pa yin no// 'di lta ste/ dper na/ grib ma snang yang mi dmigs pa de bzhin du/ bad mo de yang slang mod kyi mi dmigaso// gang gi tshe bdud sdig can gyis

47a1(tog gzungs): gtso mchog skyabasu bdag 'chi ste/ gti mug gis de bdag rmongs khyod la bros shing nongs chen bgyis// mngon gsum khyod bzhag spyan sngar de dag so sor bshags par

47a3(tog gzungs): pa de'i tshe/ yang 'gul ba bcings pa lngas bcings pa dag gis shes te/ gang gi tshe gang du yang 'gro ma nus pa de'i tshe/ bcom ldan 'das la mgon dang skyab su sems bskyed nas

47b1(tog gzungs): za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po brgya stong mang po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa lo dad pa rnams gdong / 'chi ma can gyis

49a1(tog gzungs): lha mo grub pa'i blo gros zhes bya ba des/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// 'jig rten sgron ma brlag 'gyur na/ kye hud
